for me it was with my first ever clan in an online game star wars dark forces jedi knight believe it or not the multiplayer scene was fairly intense i managed to find a really cool clan with some wonderful people i was about at the time and we branched off into other star wars games at the time too x wing vs tie fighter and others got together to chat mainly on message boards and since we didn t really have anything voice chat wise yet we mainly did text based talking in game as well it solidified what i would come to want to expect from an online gaming community friendship kindness and helpfulness was always great trying to teach new players about games too would love to hear some of your stories too always fun to think about positive gaming experiences like that
